   <script charset="utf-8" type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready( function(){
 	
 		// AUTOCOMPLETE VOLLTEXTSUCHE
 		$('.vtsfld').autocomplete('/output/autocomplete_solr_leo.php', {
 		   'minChars' : 1,
 		   'max' : 20,
 		   'scrollHeight' : 500,
 		   'width' : 350,
 		   'matchSubset' : false,
 		   'selectFirst' : false,
 		   'extraParams' : {'limit' : 30},
 		   formatItem: function(data, i, n, value) {
 			  return (data[1]) ? data[1] : data[0];
 		   },
 
 		   formatResult: function(data, value) {
 			  return data[0];
 		   }
 		})
 		.result(function(event, data, formatted) { 
 			$(this).closest('form').submit(); 
 		});	
 
 		// AUTOCOMPLETE VOLLTEXTSUCHE Volkshochschule
 		$('.vtsfld_vhs').autocomplete('/output/autocomplete_solr_vhs.php', {
 		   'minChars' : 1,
 		   'max' : 20,
 		   'scrollHeight' : 500,
 		   'width' : 350,
 		   'matchSubset' : false,
 		   'selectFirst' : false,
 		   'extraParams' : {'limit' : 30},
 		   formatItem: function(data, i, n, value) {
 			  return (data[1]) ? data[1] : data[0];
 		   },
 
 		   formatResult: function(data, value) {
 			  return data[0];
 		   }
 		})
 		.result(function(event, data, formatted) { 
 			$(this).closest('form').submit(); 
 		});	
 
 		
 	});
   </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    //Tracking-Box Opt-in
 	$(document).ready(function() {
 		var doTrack = ikiss_basic.getCookie("ikiss-tracking");
 		console.log('doTrack', doTrack);
 		if (doTrack !== false)
 			return;
 		
 		console.log('buttons', $('.tracking-box-buttons button').get());
 		
 		$('.tracking-box-wrap').slideDown();	
 		$('.tracking-box-buttons button').click(function(){
 			var tracking = $(this).data('tracking');
 			ikiss_basic.setCookie('ikiss-tracking', tracking, 365);	
 			if (window._paq) {
 				if (tracking == 1) _paq.push(['trackEvent', 'ButtonPiwikTrackingOff','click']);
 				if (tracking == -1) _paq.push(['trackEvent', 'ButtonPiwikMenuOff','click']);
 			}
 			$('.tracking-box-wrap').slideUp();
 		});	
 	});
   </script>

   <script charset="utf-8" type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready( function(){
 	
 		// AUTOCOMPLETE VOLLTEXTSUCHE
 		$('.vtsfld').autocomplete('/output/autocomplete_solr_leo.php', {
 		   'minChars' : 1,
 		   'max' : 20,
 		   'scrollHeight' : 500,
 		   'width' : 350,
 		   'matchSubset' : false,
 		   'selectFirst' : false,
 		   'extraParams' : {'limit' : 30},
 		   formatItem: function(data, i, n, value) {
 			  return (data[1]) ? data[1] : data[0];
 		   },
 
 		   formatResult: function(data, value) {
 			  return data[0];
 		   }
 		})
 		.result(function(event, data, formatted) { 
 			$(this).closest('form').submit(); 
 		});	
 
 		// AUTOCOMPLETE VOLLTEXTSUCHE Volkshochschule
 		$('.vtsfld_vhs').autocomplete('/output/autocomplete_solr_vhs.php', {
 		   'minChars' : 1,
 		   'max' : 20,
 		   'scrollHeight' : 500,
 		   'width' : 350,
 		   'matchSubset' : false,
 		   'selectFirst' : false,
 		   'extraParams' : {'limit' : 30},
 		   formatItem: function(data, i, n, value) {
 			  return (data[1]) ? data[1] : data[0];
 		   },
 
 		   formatResult: function(data, value) {
 			  return data[0];
 		   }
 		})
 		.result(function(event, data, formatted) { 
 			$(this).closest('form').submit(); 
 		});	
 
 		
 	});
   </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    //Tracking-Box Opt-in
 	$(document).ready(function() {
 		var doTrack = ikiss_basic.getCookie("ikiss-tracking");
 		console.log('doTrack', doTrack);
 		if (doTrack !== false)
 			return;
 		
 		console.log('buttons', $('.tracking-box-buttons button').get());
 		
 		$('.tracking-box-wrap').slideDown();	
 		$('.tracking-box-buttons button').click(function(){
 			var tracking = $(this).data('tracking');
 			ikiss_basic.setCookie('ikiss-tracking', tracking, 365);	
 			if (window._paq) {
 				if (tracking == 1) _paq.push(['trackEvent', 'ButtonPiwikTrackingOff','click']);
 				if (tracking == -1) _paq.push(['trackEvent', 'ButtonPiwikMenuOff','click']);
 			}
 			$('.tracking-box-wrap').slideUp();
 		});	
 	});
   </script>

   <script charset="utf-8" type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready( function(){
 	
 		// AUTOCOMPLETE VOLLTEXTSUCHE
 		$('.vtsfld').autocomplete('/output/autocomplete_solr_leo.php', {
 		   'minChars' : 1,
 		   'max' : 20,
 		   'scrollHeight' : 500,
 		   'width' : 350,
 		   'matchSubset' : false,
 		   'selectFirst' : false,
 		   'extraParams' : {'limit' : 30},
 		   formatItem: function(data, i, n, value) {
 			  return (data[1]) ? data[1] : data[0];
 		   },
 
 		   formatResult: function(data, value) {
 			  return data[0];
 		   }
 		})
 		.result(function(event, data, formatted) { 
 			$(this).closest('form').submit(); 
 		});	
 
 		// AUTOCOMPLETE VOLLTEXTSUCHE Volkshochschule
 		$('.vtsfld_vhs').autocomplete('/output/autocomplete_solr_vhs.php', {
 		   'minChars' : 1,
 		   'max' : 20,
 		   'scrollHeight' : 500,
 		   'width' : 350,
 		   'matchSubset' : false,
 		   'selectFirst' : false,
 		   'extraParams' : {'limit' : 30},
 		   formatItem: function(data, i, n, value) {
 			  return (data[1]) ? data[1] : data[0];
 		   },
 
 		   formatResult: function(data, value) {
 			  return data[0];
 		   }
 		})
 		.result(function(event, data, formatted) { 
 			$(this).closest('form').submit(); 
 		});	
 
 		
 	});
   </script>

    //Tracking-Box Opt-in
 	$(document).ready(function() {
 		var doTrack = ikiss_basic.getCookie("ikiss-tracking");
 		console.log('doTrack', doTrack);
 		if (doTrack !== false)
 			return;
 		
 		console.log('buttons', $('.tracking-box-buttons button').get());
 		
 		$('.tracking-box-wrap').slideDown();	
 		$('.tracking-box-buttons button').click(function(){
 			var tracking = $(this).data('tracking');
 			ikiss_basic.setCookie('ikiss-tracking', tracking, 365);	
 			if (window._paq) {
 				if (tracking == 1) _paq.push(['trackEvent', 'ButtonPiwikTrackingOff','click']);
 				if (tracking == -1) _paq.push(['trackEvent', 'ButtonPiwikMenuOff','click']);
 			}
 			$('.tracking-box-wrap').slideUp();
 		});	
 	});
   </script>

    $(document).ready( function(){
 	
 		// AUTOCOMPLETE VOLLTEXTSUCHE
 		$('.vtsfld').autocomplete('/output/autocomplete_solr_leo.php', {
 		   'minChars' : 1,
 		   'max' : 20,
 		   'scrollHeight' : 500,
 		   'width' : 350,
 		   'matchSubset' : false,
 		   'selectFirst' : false,
 		   'extraParams' : {'limit' : 30},
 		   formatItem: function(data, i, n, value) {
 			  return (data[1]) ? data[1] : data[0];
 		   },

 			  return data[0];
 		   }
 		})

 			$(this).closest('form').submit(); 
 		});

   <script type="text/javascript">
    //Tracking-Box Opt-in
 	$(document).ready(function() {
 		var doTrack = ikiss_basic.getCookie("ikiss-tracking");
 		console.log('doTrack', doTrack);
 		if (doTrack !== false)
 			return;
 		
 		console.log('buttons', $('.tracking-box-buttons button').get());
 		
 		$('.tracking-box-wrap').slideDown();	
 		$('.tracking-box-buttons button').click(function(){
 			var tracking = $(this).data('tracking');
 			ikiss_basic.setCookie('ikiss-tracking', tracking, 365);	
 			if (window._paq) {
 				if (tracking == 1) _paq.push(['trackEvent', 'ButtonPiwikTrackingOff','click']);
 				if (tracking == -1) _paq.push(['trackEvent', 'ButtonPiwikMenuOff','click']);
 			}
 			$('.tracking-box-wrap').slideUp();
 		});	
 	});
   </script>

    $(document).ready( function(){
 	
 		// AUTOCOMPLETE VOLLTEXTSUCHE
 		$('.vtsfld').autocomplete('/output/autocomplete_solr_leo.php', {
 		   'minChars' : 1,
 		   'max' : 20,
 		   'scrollHeight' : 500,
 		   'width' : 350,
 		   'matchSubset' : false,
 		   'selectFirst' : false,
 		   'extraParams' : {'limit' : 30},
 		   formatItem: function(data, i, n, value) {
 			  return (data[1]) ? data[1] : data[0];
 		   },
 
 		   formatResult: function(data, value) {
 			  return data[0];
 		   }
 		})
 		.result(function(event, data, formatted) { 
 			$(this).closest('form').submit(); 
 		});

   <script type="text/javascript">
    //Tracking-Box Opt-in
 	$(document).ready(function() {
 		var doTrack = ikiss_basic.getCookie("ikiss-tracking");
 		console.log('doTrack', doTrack);
 		if (doTrack !== false)
 			return;
 		
 		console.log('buttons', $('.tracking-box-buttons button').get());
 		
 		$('.tracking-box-wrap').slideDown();	
 		$('.tracking-box-buttons button').click(function(){
 			var tracking = $(this).data('tracking');
 			ikiss_basic.setCookie('ikiss-tracking', tracking, 365);	
 			if (window._paq) {
 				if (tracking == 1) _paq.push(['trackEvent', 'ButtonPiwikTrackingOff','click']);
 				if (tracking == -1) _paq.push(['trackEvent', 'ButtonPiwikMenuOff','click']);
 			}
 			$('.tracking-box-wrap').slideUp();
 		});	
 	});
   </script>
